cramps are a frequent complaint among the elderly, but these painful nocturnal awakenings can affect any age group. They typically involve the calf muscles, hamstrings, or feet, often without clear warning. The exact causes are not always known; however, \u0026lsquo;true\u0026rsquo; muscle cramps are often linked to more complex physiological triggers, including lower motor neuron diseases, metabolic imbalances, medication side effects, or even specific genetic markers, such as antibodies to voltage-gated potassium channels.\u0026nbsp;\u003cbr\u003eFor active individuals, these spasms are a common byproduct of starting a new fitness regimen. They often flare up during rest as a result of dehydration, electrolyte shifts, or the accumulation of metabolic waste within muscle tissue.\u0026nbsp;\u003cbr\u003eTo keep these cramps at bay, physiotherapists recommend a proactive approach that includes consistent hydration and a dedicated routine of warm-up and cool-down exercises, along with full-body stretching\u0026mdash;incorporating the legs, arms, and trunk\u0026mdash;both before and after every workout to help muscles remain resilient and reduce fatigue.\u003c/p\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"39:T5e0,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"\u003cp\u003eFirst of all, India lacks strict social media regulations, where only individuals qualified in a particular domain should post content relevant to their field.
